I chose a sea view premium room. Fortunately, I was arranged in the middle room on the sixth floor, facing the Beibu Gulf. 
I tried the Haikushilan Scenic Area at the foot of the mountain, and Sheraton and Guanling Villa share a beach. It is best to watch the sunset on the balcony. You can watch a grand sunset sitting on the balcony. 
The hotel breakfast is rich and delicious, the ingredients are fresh, and you can start every day with full energy. 
Dinner is served in Yuechu, a Cantonese restaurant in the hotel. The star hotel service is in place, the dishes are exquisite and delicious, the waiters patiently answer questions, and you feel at home and have good memories. 
The hotel rooms are like most seaside resort hotels, with wooden floors and soft carpets around the bed. The overall color is fresh and elegant, the bedding is delicate and soft, and the mattress is moderately soft and hard. You can get a full rest after a day of play.

Finally, after staying in other hotels for a few nights, I decided to come to the Sheraton Hotel to have a look, and then decide whether to live. The hotel is located in Guantouling, a relatively remote place in the west of Beihai. People who travel often and are picky about hotels will have an intuitive feeling. All brand hotels opened in remote places in tourist cities must have beautiful scenery. The moment the car went up the mountain and entered the exclusive road of Sheraton Guantouling Hotel, I felt that the scenery of this hotel must not be bad. Sure enough, when entering the lobby, there is an invincible sea view outside the large glass directly opposite. The service staff is professional and enthusiastic. After communicating with the young man at the front desk, they upgraded the sea view room. There is nothing to say about the room, which is standard for a seaside five-star resort hotel. The only thing is that there are no drinks or snacks in the refrigerator. If these are added and provided free of charge, the style and intimacy of the hotel will immediately be upgraded to a higher level, and it will win the favor and favor of more guests. The hotel as a whole looks like a good hotel from the restaurant to the swimming pool, and the breakfast category and taste are also up to standard. Because it belongs to the Guanglv Group, the beach is shared with the nearby Guanling Villa, and because part of the Guanling Villa is being renovated, the beach is a bit messy. But it is much better than the boiled dumplings on other beaches in Beihai. If we talk about the hotel's overall cost performance, it is incomparable with the luxury brand hotels Ritz-Carlton and EDITION, which are both owned by Marriott in Sanya. It is a standard Sheraton hotel.
